\"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain is implemented in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/ package. The architecture consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. **Webhook Admission Controller (Generic Framework):**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go contains the core Webhook struct that coordinates the entire admission process. The Webhook.Dispatch() method is the central entry point that orchestrates the chain.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go defines the Source, Dispatcher, VersionedAttributeAccessor, and WebhookInvocation interfaces that form the contract for the webhook system.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go also implements ShouldCallHook() which determines whether a webhook should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions.\\n\\n2. **Webhook Plugins (Entry Points):**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go implements the MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin that handles mutating webhook admission. Its Admit() method invokes the generic webhook's Dispatch() method.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go implements the ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin that handles validating webhook admission. Its Validate() method invokes the generic webhook's Dispatch() method.\\n\\n3. **Webhook Call Dispatch (Webhook Invocation Chain):**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go implements mutatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to mutating webhooks sequentially. The Dispatch() method iterates through applicable webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each. It handles patch application, mutation tracking, reinvocation of webhooks when objects are mutated, and aggregates audit annotations.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go implements validatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to validating webhooks in parallel using goroutines. The Dispatch() method spawns concurrent webhook calls and aggregates validation errors. It collects all errors and returns the first one as a failure.\\n   - Both dispatchers inherit from the generic Dispatcher interface and use webhookutil.ClientManager for REST calls to webhook servers.\\n\\n4. **Admission Response Aggregation:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go provides CreateAdmissionObjects() to marshal admission requests and VerifyAdmissionResponse() to validate and extract response data. The VerifyAdmissionResponse() function aggregates response fields including patches, audit annotations, warnings, and rejection status.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go aggregates patches from mutating webhooks using JSON patch operations and applies them sequentially to the object. It also aggregates audit annotations about mutations and failed-open scenarios.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go aggregates validation results by collecting errors from parallel webhook calls and returning the first error, while logging other errors.\\n\\n5. **Webhook Configuration Management:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go implements NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager() which serves as a Source of mutating webhooks from MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go implements NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager() which serves as a Source of validating webhooks from ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources.\\n   - The Dispatch() method iterates through applicable webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each. It handles patch application, mutation tracking, reinvocation of webhooks when objects are mutated, and aggregates audit annotations.\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go implements validatingDispatcher which dispatches admission requests to validating webhooks in parallel using goroutines. The Dispatch() method spawns concurrent webhook calls and aggregates validation errors. It collects all errors and returns the first one as a failure.\\n   - Both dispatchers inherit from the generic Dispatcher interface and use webhookutil.ClientManager for REST calls to webhook servers.\\n\\n4. **Admission Response Aggregation:**\\n   - staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go provides CreateAdmissionObjects() to marshal admission requests and VerifyAdmissionResponse() to validate and extract response data.
